    FROM [collection_history] AS [c]
    WHERE ([c].[call_by] = @__reqUser_Id_0) AND ((CONVERT(date, [c].[history_date]) >= @__dst_1) AND (CONVERT(date, [c].[history_date]) <= @__ded_2))
    ORDER BY [c].[id] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_3 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_4 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [collection_add_contact] AS [c0] ON [t].[add_id] = [c0].[id]

LEFT JOIN [rfproduct] AS [r1] ON [m].[product] = [r1].[id]

ORDER BY [t].[id] DESC
